# Emby Server API
Version: 4.1.1.0
Description: Explore the Emby Server API

## GET /Artists
**Summary**: Gets all artists from a given item, folder, or the entire library
**Details**: Requires authentication as user
**Parameters**:
- `ArtistType` (query string): Artist or AlbumArtist
- `MaxOfficialRating` (query string): Optional filter by maximum official rating (PG, PG-13, TV-MA, etc).
- `HasThemeSong` (query boolean): Optional filter by items with theme songs.
- `HasThemeVideo` (query boolean): Optional filter by items with theme videos.
- `HasSubtitles` (query boolean): Optional filter by items with subtitles.
- `HasSpecialFeature` (query boolean): Optional filter by items with special features.
- `HasTrailer` (query boolean): Optional filter by items with trailers.
- `AdjacentTo` (query string): Optional. Return items that are siblings of a supplied item.
- `MinIndexNumber` (query integer): Optional filter by minimum index number.
- `MinPlayers` (query integer): Optional filter by minimum number of game players.
- `MaxPlayers` (query integer): Optional filter by maximum number of game players.
- `ParentIndexNumber` (query integer): Optional filter by parent index number.
- `HasParentalRating` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that have or do not have a parental rating
- `IsHD` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are HD or not.
- `LocationTypes` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on LocationType. This allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `ExcludeLocationTypes` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on LocationType. This allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `IsMissing` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are missing episodes or not.
- `IsUnaired` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are unaired episodes or not.
- `MinCommunityRating` (query number): Optional filter by minimum community rating.
- `MinCriticRating` (query number): Optional filter by minimum critic rating.
- `AiredDuringSeason` (query integer): Gets all episodes that aired during a season, including specials.
- `MinPremiereDate` (query string): Optional. The minimum premiere date. Format = ISO
- `MinDateLastSaved` (query string): Optional. The minimum premiere date. Format = ISO
- `MinDateLastSavedForUser` (query string): Optional. The minimum premiere date. Format = ISO
- `MaxPremiereDate` (query string): Optional. The maximum premiere date. Format = ISO
- `HasOverview` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that have an overview or not.
- `HasImdbId` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that have an imdb id or not.
- `HasTmdbId` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that have a tmdb id or not.
- `HasTvdbId` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that have a tvdb id or not.
- `ExcludeItemIds` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered by exxcluding item ids. This allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `StartIndex` (query integer): Optional. The record index to start at. All items with a lower index will be dropped from the results.
- `Limit` (query integer): Optional. The maximum number of records to return
- `Recursive` (query boolean): When searching within folders, this determines whether or not the search will be recursive. true/false
- `SortOrder` (query string): Sort Order - Ascending,Descending
- `ParentId` (query string): Specify this to localize the search to a specific item or folder. Omit to use the root
- `Fields` (query string): Optional. Specify additional fields of information to return in the output. This allows multiple, comma delimeted. Options: Budget, Chapters, DateCreated, Genres, HomePageUrl, IndexOptions, MediaStreams, Overview, ParentId, Path, People, ProviderIds, PrimaryImageAspectRatio, Revenue, SortName, Studios, Taglines
- `ExcludeItemTypes` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on item type. This allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `IncludeItemTypes` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on item type. This allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `AnyProviderIdEquals` (query string): Optional. If specified, result will be filtered to contain only items which match at least one of the specified IDs. Each provider ID must be in the form 'prov.id', e.g. 'imdb.tt123456'. This allows multiple, comma delimeted value pairs.
- `Filters` (query string): Optional. Specify additional filters to apply. This allows multiple, comma delimeted. Options: IsFolder, IsNotFolder, IsUnplayed, IsPlayed, IsFavorite, IsResumable, Likes, Dislikes
- `IsFavorite` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are marked as favorite, or not.
- `IsMovie` (query boolean): Optional filter for movies.
- `IsSeries` (query boolean): Optional filter for movies.
- `IsNews` (query boolean): Optional filter for news.
- `IsKids` (query boolean): Optional filter for kids.
- `IsSports` (query boolean): Optional filter for sports.
- `MediaTypes` (query string): Optional filter by MediaType. Allows multiple, comma delimited.
- `ImageTypes` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on those containing image types. This allows multiple, comma delimited.
- `SortBy` (query string): Optional. Specify one or more sort orders, comma delimeted. Options: Album, AlbumArtist, Artist, Budget, CommunityRating, CriticRating, DateCreated, DatePlayed, PlayCount, PremiereDate, ProductionYear, SortName, Random, Revenue, Runtime
- `IsPlayed` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are played, or not.
- `Genres` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on genre. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `OfficialRatings` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on OfficialRating. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `Tags` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on tag. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `Years` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on production year. This allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `EnableImages` (query boolean): Optional, include image information in output
- `EnableUserData` (query boolean): Optional, include user data
- `ImageTypeLimit` (query integer): Optional, the max number of images to return, per image type
- `EnableImageTypes` (query string): Optional. The image types to include in the output.
- `Person` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered to include only those containing the specified person.
- `PersonIds` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered to include only those containing the specified person.
- `PersonTypes` (query string): Optional. If specified, along with Person, results will be filtered to include only those containing the specified person and PersonType. Allows multiple, comma-delimited
- `Studios` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on studio. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `StudioIds` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on studio. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `Artists` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on artist. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `ArtistIds` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on artist. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `Albums` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on album. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `Ids` (query string): Optional. If specific items are needed, specify a list of item id's to retrieve. This allows multiple, comma delimited.
- `VideoTypes` (query string): Optional filter by VideoType (videofile, dvd, bluray, iso). Allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `Containers` (query string): Optional filter by Container. Allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `AudioCodecs` (query string): Optional filter by AudioCodec. Allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `VideoCodecs` (query string): Optional filter by VideoCodec. Allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `SubtitleCodecs` (query string): Optional filter by SubtitleCodec. Allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `Path` (query string): Optional filter by Path.
- `UserId` (query string): User Id
- `MinOfficialRating` (query string): Optional filter by minimum official rating (PG, PG-13, TV-MA, etc).
- `IsLocked` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are locked.
- `IsPlaceHolder` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are placeholders
- `HasOfficialRating` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that have official ratings
- `GroupItemsIntoCollections` (query boolean): Whether or not to hide items behind their boxsets.
- `Is3D` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are 3D, or not.
- `SeriesStatus` (query string): Optional filter by Series Status. Allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `NameStartsWithOrGreater` (query string): Optional filter by items whose name is sorted equally or greater than a given input string.
- `NameStartsWith` (query string): Optional filter by items whose name is sorted equally than a given input string.
- `NameLessThan` (query string): Optional filter by items whose name is equally or lesser than a given input string.

## GET /AudioCodecs
**Summary**: Gets items based on a query.
**Details**: No authentication required
**Parameters**:
- `ArtistType` (query string): Artist or AlbumArtist
- `MaxOfficialRating` (query string): Optional filter by maximum official rating (PG, PG-13, TV-MA, etc).
- `HasThemeSong` (query boolean): Optional filter by items with theme songs.
- `HasThemeVideo` (query boolean): Optional filter by items with theme videos.
- `HasSubtitles` (query boolean): Optional filter by items with subtitles.
- `HasSpecialFeature` (query boolean): Optional filter by items with special features.
- `HasTrailer` (query boolean): Optional filter by items with trailers.
- `AdjacentTo` (query string): Optional. Return items that are siblings of a supplied item.
- `MinIndexNumber` (query integer): Optional filter by minimum index number.
- `MinPlayers` (query integer): Optional filter by minimum number of game players.
- `MaxPlayers` (query integer): Optional filter by maximum number of game players.
- `ParentIndexNumber` (query integer): Optional filter by parent index number.
- `HasParentalRating` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that have or do not have a parental rating
- `IsHD` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are HD or not.
- `LocationTypes` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on LocationType. This allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `ExcludeLocationTypes` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on LocationType. This allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `IsMissing` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are missing episodes or not.
- `IsUnaired` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are unaired episodes or not.
- `MinCommunityRating` (query number): Optional filter by minimum community rating.
- `MinCriticRating` (query number): Optional filter by minimum critic rating.
- `AiredDuringSeason` (query integer): Gets all episodes that aired during a season, including specials.
- `MinPremiereDate` (query string): Optional. The minimum premiere date. Format = ISO
- `MinDateLastSaved` (query string): Optional. The minimum premiere date. Format = ISO
- `MinDateLastSavedForUser` (query string): Optional. The minimum premiere date. Format = ISO
- `MaxPremiereDate` (query string): Optional. The maximum premiere date. Format = ISO
- `HasOverview` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that have an overview or not.
- `HasImdbId` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that have an imdb id or not.
- `HasTmdbId` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that have a tmdb id or not.
- `HasTvdbId` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that have a tvdb id or not.
- `ExcludeItemIds` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered by exxcluding item ids. This allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `StartIndex` (query integer): Optional. The record index to start at. All items with a lower index will be dropped from the results.
- `Limit` (query integer): Optional. The maximum number of records to return
- `Recursive` (query boolean): When searching within folders, this determines whether or not the search will be recursive. true/false
- `SortOrder` (query string): Sort Order - Ascending,Descending
- `ParentId` (query string): Specify this to localize the search to a specific item or folder. Omit to use the root
- `Fields` (query string): Optional. Specify additional fields of information to return in the output. This allows multiple, comma delimeted. Options: Budget, Chapters, DateCreated, Genres, HomePageUrl, IndexOptions, MediaStreams, Overview, ParentId, Path, People, ProviderIds, PrimaryImageAspectRatio, Revenue, SortName, Studios, Taglines
- `ExcludeItemTypes` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on item type. This allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `IncludeItemTypes` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on item type. This allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `AnyProviderIdEquals` (query string): Optional. If specified, result will be filtered to contain only items which match at least one of the specified IDs. Each provider ID must be in the form 'prov.id', e.g. 'imdb.tt123456'. This allows multiple, comma delimeted value pairs.
- `Filters` (query string): Optional. Specify additional filters to apply. This allows multiple, comma delimeted. Options: IsFolder, IsNotFolder, IsUnplayed, IsPlayed, IsFavorite, IsResumable, Likes, Dislikes
- `IsFavorite` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are marked as favorite, or not.
- `IsMovie` (query boolean): Optional filter for movies.
- `IsSeries` (query boolean): Optional filter for movies.
- `IsNews` (query boolean): Optional filter for news.
- `IsKids` (query boolean): Optional filter for kids.
- `IsSports` (query boolean): Optional filter for sports.
- `MediaTypes` (query string): Optional filter by MediaType. Allows multiple, comma delimited.
- `ImageTypes` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on those containing image types. This allows multiple, comma delimited.
- `SortBy` (query string): Optional. Specify one or more sort orders, comma delimeted. Options: Album, AlbumArtist, Artist, Budget, CommunityRating, CriticRating, DateCreated, DatePlayed, PlayCount, PremiereDate, ProductionYear, SortName, Random, Revenue, Runtime
- `IsPlayed` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are played, or not.
- `Genres` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on genre. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `OfficialRatings` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on OfficialRating. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `Tags` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on tag. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `Years` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on production year. This allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `EnableImages` (query boolean): Optional, include image information in output
- `EnableUserData` (query boolean): Optional, include user data
- `ImageTypeLimit` (query integer): Optional, the max number of images to return, per image type
- `EnableImageTypes` (query string): Optional. The image types to include in the output.
- `Person` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered to include only those containing the specified person.
- `PersonIds` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered to include only those containing the specified person.
- `PersonTypes` (query string): Optional. If specified, along with Person, results will be filtered to include only those containing the specified person and PersonType. Allows multiple, comma-delimited
- `Studios` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on studio. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `StudioIds` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on studio. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `Artists` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on artist. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `ArtistIds` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on artist. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `Albums` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on album. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `Ids` (query string): Optional. If specific items are needed, specify a list of item id's to retrieve. This allows multiple, comma delimited.
- `VideoTypes` (query string): Optional filter by VideoType (videofile, dvd, bluray, iso). Allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `Containers` (query string): Optional filter by Container. Allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `AudioCodecs` (query string): Optional filter by AudioCodec. Allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `VideoCodecs` (query string): Optional filter by VideoCodec. Allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `SubtitleCodecs` (query string): Optional filter by SubtitleCodec. Allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `Path` (query string): Optional filter by Path.
- `UserId` (query string): User Id
- `MinOfficialRating` (query string): Optional filter by minimum official rating (PG, PG-13, TV-MA, etc).
- `IsLocked` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are locked.
- `IsPlaceHolder` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are placeholders
- `HasOfficialRating` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that have official ratings
- `GroupItemsIntoCollections` (query boolean): Whether or not to hide items behind their boxsets.
- `Is3D` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are 3D, or not.
- `SeriesStatus` (query string): Optional filter by Series Status. Allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `NameStartsWithOrGreater` (query string): Optional filter by items whose name is sorted equally or greater than a given input string.
- `NameStartsWith` (query string): Optional filter by items whose name is sorted equally than a given input string.
- `NameLessThan` (query string): Optional filter by items whose name is equally or lesser than a given input string.

## GET /Channels
**Summary**: Gets available channels
**Details**: Requires authentication as user
**Parameters**:
- `UserId` (query string): User Id
- `StartIndex` (query integer): Optional. The record index to start at. All items with a lower index will be dropped from the results.
- `Limit` (query integer): Optional. The maximum number of records to return

## POST /Collections
**Summary**: Creates a new collection
**Details**: Requires authentication as user
**Parameters**:
- `IsLocked` (query boolean): Whether or not to lock the new collection.
- `Name` (query string): The name of the new collection.
- `ParentId` (query string): Optional - create the collection within a specific folder
- `Ids` (query string): Item Ids to add to the collection

## GET /Containers
**Summary**: Gets items based on a query.
**Details**: No authentication required
**Parameters**:

## GET /Devices
**Summary**: Gets all devices
**Details**: Requires authentication as administrator

## DELETE /Devices
**Summary**: Deletes a device
**Details**: No authentication required
**Parameters**:
- `Id`* (query string): Device Id

## GET /GameGenres
**Summary**: Gets all Game genres from a given item, folder, or the entire library
**Details**: Requires authentication as user
**Parameters**:
- `ArtistType` (query string): Artist or AlbumArtist
- `MaxOfficialRating` (query string): Optional filter by maximum official rating (PG, PG-13, TV-MA, etc).
- `HasThemeSong` (query boolean): Optional filter by items with theme songs.
- `HasThemeVideo` (query boolean): Optional filter by items with theme videos.
- `HasSubtitles` (query boolean): Optional filter by items with subtitles.
- `HasSpecialFeature` (query boolean): Optional filter by items with special features.
- `HasTrailer` (query boolean): Optional filter by items with trailers.
- `AdjacentTo` (query string): Optional. Return items that are siblings of a supplied item.
- `MinIndexNumber` (query integer): Optional filter by minimum index number.
- `MinPlayers` (query integer): Optional filter by minimum number of game players.
- `MaxPlayers` (query integer): Optional filter by maximum number of game players.
- `ParentIndexNumber` (query integer): Optional filter by parent index number.
- `HasParentalRating` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that have or do not have a parental rating
- `IsHD` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are HD or not.
- `LocationTypes` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on LocationType. This allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `ExcludeLocationTypes` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on LocationType. This allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `IsMissing` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are missing episodes or not.
- `IsUnaired` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are unaired episodes or not.
- `MinCommunityRating` (query number): Optional filter by minimum community rating.
- `MinCriticRating` (query number): Optional filter by minimum critic rating.
- `AiredDuringSeason` (query integer): Gets all episodes that aired during a season, including specials.
- `MinPremiereDate` (query string): Optional. The minimum premiere date. Format = ISO
- `MinDateLastSaved` (query string): Optional. The minimum premiere date. Format = ISO
- `MinDateLastSavedForUser` (query string): Optional. The minimum premiere date. Format = ISO
- `MaxPremiereDate` (query string): Optional. The maximum premiere date. Format = ISO
- `HasOverview` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that have an overview or not.
- `HasImdbId` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that have an imdb id or not.
- `HasTmdbId` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that have a tmdb id or not.
- `HasTvdbId` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that have a tvdb id or not.

Options: Budget, Chapters, DateCreated, Genres, HomePageUrl, IndexOptions, MediaStreams, Overview, ParentId, Path, People, ProviderIds, PrimaryImageAspectRatio, Revenue, SortName, Studios, Taglines

- `IncludeItemTypes` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on item type. This allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `AnyProviderIdEquals` (query string): Optional. If specified, result will be filtered to contain only items which match at least one of the specified IDs. Each provider ID must be in the form 'prov.id', e.g. 'imdb.tt123456'. This allows multiple, comma delimeted value pairs.

## GET /Items/{Id}/Images/{Type}/{Index}/{Tag}/{Format}/{MaxWidth}/{MaxHeight}/{PercentPlayed}/{UnplayedCount}
**Summary**: No summary
**Details**: No authentication required
**Parameters**:
- `Id`* (path string): Item Id
- `MaxWidth`* (path integer): The maximum image width to return.
- `MaxHeight`* (path integer): The maximum image height to return.
- `Width` (query integer): The fixed image width to return.
- `Height` (query integer): The fixed image height to return.
- `Quality` (query integer): Optional quality setting, from 0-100. Defaults to 90 and should suffice in most cases.
- `Tag`* (path string): Optional. Supply the cache tag from the item object to receive strong caching headers.
- `CropWhitespace` (query boolean): Specify if whitespace should be cropped out of the image. True/False. If unspecified, whitespace will be cropped from logos and clear art.
- `EnableImageEnhancers` (query boolean): Enable or disable image enhancers such as cover art.
- `Format`* (path string): Determines the output foramt of the image - original,gif,jpg,png
- `AddPlayedIndicator` (query boolean): Optional. Add a played indicator
- `PercentPlayed`* (path number): Optional percent to render for the percent played overlay
- `UnplayedCount`* (path integer): Optional unplayed count overlay to render
- `BackgroundColor` (query string): Optional. Apply a background color for transparent images.
- `ForegroundLayer` (query string): Optional. Apply a foreground layer on top of the image.
- `Type`* (path string): Image Type
- `Index`* (path integer): Image Index

- `HasImdbId` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that have an imdb id or not.
- `HasTmdbId` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that have a tmdb id or not.
- `HasTvdbId` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that have a tvdb id or not.
- `ExcludeItemIds` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered by exxcluding item ids. This allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `StartIndex` (query integer): Optional. The record index to start at. All items with a lower index will be dropped from the results.
- `Limit` (query integer): Optional. The maximum number of records to return
- `Recursive` (query boolean): When searching within folders, this determines whether or not the search will be recursive. true/false
- `SortOrder` (query string): Sort Order - Ascending,Descending
- `ParentId` (query string): Specify this to localize the search to a specific item or folder. Omit to use the root
- `Fields` (query string): Optional. Specify additional fields of information to return in the output. This allows multiple, comma delimeted. Options: Budget, Chapters, DateCreated, Genres, HomePageUrl, IndexOptions, MediaStreams, Overview, ParentId, Path, People, ProviderIds, PrimaryImageAspectRatio, Revenue, SortName, Studios, Taglines
- `ExcludeItemTypes` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on item type. This allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `IncludeItemTypes` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on item type. This allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `AnyProviderIdEquals` (query string): Optional. If specified, result will be filtered to contain only items which match at least one of the specified IDs. Each provider ID must be in the form 'prov.id', e.g. 'imdb.tt123456'. This allows multiple, comma delimeted value pairs.
- `Filters` (query string): Optional. Specify additional filters to apply. This allows multiple, comma delimeted. Options: IsFolder, IsNotFolder, IsUnplayed, IsPlayed, IsFavorite, IsResumable, Likes, Dislikes
- `IsFavorite` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are marked as favorite, or not.

- `IsSeries` (query boolean): Optional filter for movies.
- `IsNews` (query boolean): Optional filter for news.

- `ImageTypes` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on those containing image types. This allows multiple, comma delimited.

- `EnableImageTypes` (query string): Optional. The image types to include in the output.

- `HasSubtitles` (query boolean): Optional filter by items with subtitles.
- `HasSpecialFeature` (query boolean): Optional filter by items with special features.
- `HasTrailer` (query boolean): Optional filter by items with trailers.
- `AdjacentTo` (query string): Optional. Return items that are siblings of a supplied item.

- `MinPlayers` (query integer): Optional filter by minimum number of game players.
- `MaxPlayers` (query integer): Optional filter by maximum number of game players.
- `ParentIndexNumber` (query integer): Optional filter by parent index number.
- `HasParentalRating` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that have or do not have a parental rating
- `IsHD` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are HD or not.
- `LocationTypes` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on LocationType. This allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `ExcludeLocationTypes` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on LocationType. This allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `IsMissing` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are missing episodes or not.
- `IsUnaired` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are unaired episodes or not.
- `MinCommunityRating` (query number): Optional filter by minimum community rating.
- `MinCriticRating` (query number): Optional filter by minimum critic rating.
- `AiredDuringSeason` (query integer): Gets all episodes that aired during a season, including specials.
- `MinPremiereDate` (query string): Optional. The minimum premiere date. Format = ISO
- `MinDateLastSaved` (query string): Optional. The minimum premiere date. Format = ISO
- `MinDateLastSavedForUser` (query string): Optional. The minimum premiere date. Format = ISO
- `MaxPremiereDate` (query string): Optional. The maximum premiere date. Format = ISO
- `HasOverview` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that have an overview or not.
- `HasImdbId` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that have an imdb id or not.
- `HasTmdbId` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that have a tmdb id or not.
- `HasTvdbId` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that have a tvdb id or not.
- `ExcludeItemIds` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered by exxcluding item ids. This allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `StartIndex` (query integer): Optional. The record index to start at. All items with a lower index will be dropped from the results.
- `Limit` (query integer): Optional. The maximum number of records to return
- `Recursive` (query boolean): When searching within folders, this determines whether or not the search will be recursive. true/false
- `SortOrder` (query string): Sort Order - Ascending,Descending
- `ParentId` (query string): Specify this to localize the search to a specific item or folder. Omit to use the root
- `Fields` (query string): Optional. Specify additional fields of information to return in the output. This allows multiple, comma delimeted. Options: Budget, Chapters, DateCreated, Genres, HomePageUrl, IndexOptions, MediaStreams, Overview, ParentId, Path, People, ProviderIds, PrimaryImageAspectRatio, Revenue, SortName, Studios, Taglines
- `ExcludeItemTypes` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on item type. This allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `IncludeItemTypes` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on item type. This allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `AnyProviderIdEquals` (query string): Optional. If specified, result will be filtered to contain only items which match at least one of the specified IDs. Each provider ID must be in the form 'prov.id', e.g. 'imdb.tt123456'. This allows multiple, comma delimeted value pairs.
- `Filters` (query string): Optional. Specify additional filters to apply. This allows multiple, comma delimeted. Options: IsFolder, IsNotFolder, IsUnplayed, IsPlayed, IsFavorite, IsResumable, Likes, Dislikes
- `IsFavorite` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are marked as favorite, or not.
- `IsMovie` (query boolean): Optional filter for movies.
- `IsSeries` (query boolean): Optional filter for movies.
- `IsNews` (query boolean): Optional filter for news.
- `IsKids` (query boolean): Optional filter for kids.
- `IsSports` (query boolean): Optional filter for sports.
- `MediaTypes` (query string): Optional filter by MediaType. Allows multiple, comma delimited.
- `ImageTypes` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on those containing image types. This allows multiple, comma delimited.
- `SortBy` (query string): Optional. Specify one or more sort orders, comma delimeted. Options: Album, AlbumArtist, Artist, Budget, CommunityRating, CriticRating, DateCreated, DatePlayed, PlayCount, PremiereDate, ProductionYear, SortName, Random, Revenue, Runtime
- `IsPlayed` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are played, or not.
- `Genres` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on genre. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `OfficialRatings` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on OfficialRating. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `Tags` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on tag. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `Years` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on production year. This allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `EnableImages` (query boolean): Optional, include image information in output
- `EnableUserData` (query boolean): Optional, include user data
- `ImageTypeLimit` (query integer): Optional, the max number of images to return, per image type
- `EnableImageTypes` (query string): Optional. The image types to include in the output.
- `Person` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered to include only those containing the specified person.
- `PersonIds` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered to include only those containing the specified person.
- `PersonTypes` (query string): Optional. If specified, along with Person, results will be filtered to include only those containing the specified person and PersonType. Allows multiple, comma-delimited
- `Studios` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on studio. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `StudioIds` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on studio. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `Artists` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on artist. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.

- `ReportColumns` (query string): Optional. The columns to show.

## POST /Users/AuthenticateByName
**Summary**: Authenticates a user
**Details**: Authenticate a user by nane and password. A 200 status code indicates success, while anything in the 400 or 500 range indicates failure --- No authentication required
**Parameters**:
- `X-Emby-Authorization`* (header string): The authorization header can be either named 'Authorization' or 'X-Emby-Authorization'. It must be of the following schema: Emby UserId="(guid)", Client="(string)", Device="(string)", DeviceId="(string)", Version="string", Token="(string)" Please consult the documentation for further details.
**Body**: application/json -> Requires object `AuthenticateUserByName`
**Body**: application/xml -> Requires object `AuthenticateUserByName`

## GET /Audio/{Id}/stream.{Container}
**Summary**: Gets an audio stream
**Details**: No authentication required
**Parameters**:
- `DeviceProfileId` (query string): Optional. The dlna device profile id to utilize.
- `Id`* (path string): Item Id
- `DeviceId` (query string): The device id of the client requesting. Used to stop encoding processes when needed.
- `Container`* (path string): Container
- `AudioCodec` (query string): Optional. Specify a audio codec to encode to, e.g. mp3. If omitted the server will auto-select using the url's extension. Options: aac, mp3, vorbis, wma.
- `EnableAutoStreamCopy` (query boolean): Whether or not to allow automatic stream copy if requested values match the original source. Defaults to true.
- `AudioSampleRate` (query integer): Optional. Specify a specific audio sample rate, e.g. 44100
- `AudioBitRate` (query integer): Optional. Specify an audio bitrate to encode to, e.g. 128000. If omitted this will be left to encoder defaults.
- `AudioChannels` (query integer): Optional. Specify a specific number of audio channels to encode to, e.g. 2
- `MaxAudioChannels` (query integer): Optional. Specify a maximum number of audio channels to encode to, e.g. 2
- `Static` (query boolean): Optional. If true, the original file will be streamed statically without any encoding. Use either no url extension or the original file extension. true/false
- `Profile` (query string): Optional. Specify a specific h264 profile, e.g. main, baseline, high.
- `Level` (query string): Optional. Specify a level for the h264 profile, e.g. 3, 3.1.
- `Framerate` (query number): Optional. A specific video framerate to encode to, e.g. 23.976. Generally this should be omitted unless the device has specific requirements.
- `MaxFramerate` (query number): Optional. A specific maximum video framerate to encode to, e.g. 23.976. Generally this should be omitted unless the device has specific requirements.
- `CopyTimestamps` (query boolean): Whether or not to copy timestamps when transcoding with an offset. Defaults to false.
- `StartTimeTicks` (query integer): Optional. Specify a starting offset, in ticks. 1 tick = 10000 ms
- `Width` (query integer): Optional. The fixed horizontal resolution of the encoded video.
- `Height` (query integer): Optional. The fixed vertical resolution of the encoded video.
- `MaxWidth` (query integer): Optional. The maximum horizontal resolution of the encoded video.
- `MaxHeight` (query integer): Optional. The maximum vertical resolution of the encoded video.
- `VideoBitRate` (query integer): Optional. Specify a video bitrate to encode to, e.g. 500000. If omitted this will be left to encoder defaults.
- `SubtitleStreamIndex` (query integer): Optional. The index of the subtitle stream to use. If omitted no subtitles will be used.
- `SubtitleMethod` (query string): Optional. Specify the subtitle delivery method.
- `MaxRefFrames` (query integer): Optional.
- `MaxVideoBitDepth` (query integer): Optional.
- `VideoCodec` (query string): Optional. Specify a video codec to encode to, e.g. h264. If omitted the server will auto-select using the url's extension. Options: h264, mpeg4, theora, vpx, wmv.
- `AudioStreamIndex` (query integer): Optional. The index of the audio stream to use. If omitted the first audio stream will be used.
- `VideoStreamIndex` (query integer): Optional. The index of the video stream to use. If omitted the first video stream will be used.

**Parameters**:
- `DeviceProfileId` (query string): Optional. The dlna device profile id to utilize.
- `Id`* (path string): Item Id
- `DeviceId` (query string): The device id of the client requesting. Used to stop encoding processes when needed.
- `Container`* (query string): Container
- `AudioCodec` (query string): Optional. Specify a audio codec to encode to, e.g. mp3. If omitted the server will auto-select using the url's extension. Options: aac, mp3, vorbis, wma.
- `EnableAutoStreamCopy` (query boolean): Whether or not to allow automatic stream copy if requested values match the original source. Defaults to true.
- `AudioSampleRate` (query integer): Optional. Specify a specific audio sample rate, e.g. 44100
- `AudioBitRate` (query integer): Optional. Specify an audio bitrate to encode to, e.g. 128000. If omitted this will be left to encoder defaults.
- `AudioChannels` (query integer): Optional. Specify a specific number of audio channels to encode to, e.g. 2
- `MaxAudioChannels` (query integer): Optional. Specify a maximum number of audio channels to encode to, e.g. 2
- `Static` (query boolean): Optional. If true, the original file will be streamed statically without any encoding. Use either no url extension or the original file extension. true/false
- `Profile` (query string): Optional. Specify a specific h264 profile, e.g. main, baseline, high.
- `Level` (query string): Optional. Specify a level for the h264 profile, e.g. 3, 3.1.
- `Framerate` (query number): Optional. A specific video framerate to encode to, e.g. 23.976. Generally this should be omitted unless the device has specific requirements.
- `MaxFramerate` (query number): Optional. A specific maximum video framerate to encode to, e.g. 23.976. Generally this should be omitted unless the device has specific requirements.
- `CopyTimestamps` (query boolean): Whether or not to copy timestamps when transcoding with an offset. Defaults to false.
- `StartTimeTicks` (query integer): Optional. Specify a starting offset, in ticks. 1 tick = 10000 ms
- `Width` (query integer): Optional. The fixed horizontal resolution of the encoded video.
- `Height` (query integer): Optional. The fixed vertical resolution of the encoded video.
- `MaxWidth` (query integer): Optional. The maximum horizontal resolution of the encoded video.
- `MaxHeight` (query integer): Optional. The maximum vertical resolution of the encoded video.
- `VideoBitRate` (query integer): Optional. Specify a video bitrate to encode to, e.g. 500000. If omitted this will be left to encoder defaults.
- `SubtitleStreamIndex` (query integer): Optional. The index of the subtitle stream to use. If omitted no subtitles will be used.
- `SubtitleMethod` (query string): Optional. Specify the subtitle delivery method.
- `MaxRefFrames` (query integer): Optional.
- `MaxVideoBitDepth` (query integer): Optional.
- `VideoCodec` (query string): Optional. Specify a video codec to encode to, e.g. h264. If omitted the server will auto-select using the url's extension. Options: h264, mpeg4, theora, vpx, wmv.
- `AudioStreamIndex` (query integer): Optional. The index of the audio stream to use. If omitted the first audio stream will be used.
- `VideoStreamIndex` (query integer): Optional. The index of the video stream to use. If omitted the first video stream will be used.

- `EnableUserData` (query boolean): Optional, include user data
- `ImageTypeLimit` (query integer): Optional, the max number of images to return, per image type
- `EnableImageTypes` (query string): Optional. The image types to include in the output.
- `UserId` (query string): Optional. Filter by user id, and attach user data
- `Limit` (query integer): Optional. The maximum number of records to return
- `Fields` (query string): Optional. Specify additional fields of information to return in the output. This allows multiple, comma delimeted. ## GET /Reports/Items/Download
**Summary**: Downloads report
**Details**: No authentication required
**Parameters**:
- `MaxOfficialRating` (query string): Optional filter by maximum official rating (PG, PG-13, TV-MA, etc).
- `HasThemeSong` (query boolean): Optional filter by items with theme songs.
- `HasThemeVideo` (query boolean): Optional filter by items with theme videos.
- `HasSubtitles` (query boolean): Optional filter by items with subtitles.
- `HasSpecialFeature` (query boolean): Optional filter by items with special features.
- `HasTrailer` (query boolean): Optional filter by items with trailers.
- `AdjacentTo` (query string): Optional. Return items that are siblings of a supplied item.
- `MinIndexNumber` (query integer): Optional filter by minimum index number.
- `MinPlayers` (query integer): Optional filter by minimum number of game players.
- `MaxPlayers` (query integer): Optional filter by maximum number of game players.
- `ParentIndexNumber` (query integer): Optional filter by parent index number.
- `HasParentalRating` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that have or do not have a parental rating
- `IsHD` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are HD or not.
- `LocationTypes` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on LocationType. This allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `ExcludeLocationTypes` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on LocationType. This allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `IsMissing` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are missing episodes or not.
- `IsUnaired` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are unaired episodes or not.
- `MinCommunityRating` (query number): Optional filter by minimum community rating.
- `MinCriticRating` (query number): Optional filter by minimum critic rating.
- `AiredDuringSeason` (query integer): Gets all episodes that aired during a season, including specials.
- `MinPremiereDate` (query string): Optional. The minimum premiere date. Format = ISO
- `MinDateLastSaved` (query string): Optional. The minimum premiere date. Format = ISO
- `MinDateLastSavedForUser` (query string): Optional. The minimum premiere date. Format = ISO
- `MaxPremiereDate` (query string): Optional. The maximum premiere date. Format = ISO
- `HasOverview` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that have an overview or not.
- `HasImdbId` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that have an imdb id or not.
- `HasTmdbId` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that have a tmdb id or not.
- `HasTvdbId` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that have a tvdb id or not.
- `ExcludeItemIds` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered by exxcluding item ids. This allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `StartIndex` (query integer): Optional. The record index to start at. All items with a lower index will be dropped from the results.
- `Limit` (query integer): Optional. The maximum number of records to return
- `Recursive` (query boolean): When searching within folders, this determines whether or not the search will be recursive. true/false
- `SortOrder` (query string): Sort Order - Ascending,Descending
- `ParentId` (query string): Specify this to localize the search to a specific item or folder. Omit to use the root
- `Fields` (query string): Optional. Specify additional fields of information to return in the output. This allows multiple, comma delimeted. Options: Budget, Chapters, DateCreated, Genres, HomePageUrl, IndexOptions, MediaStreams, Overview, ParentId, Path, People, ProviderIds, PrimaryImageAspectRatio, Revenue, SortName, Studios, Taglines
- `ExcludeItemTypes` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on item type. This allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `IncludeItemTypes` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on item type. This allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `Filters` (query string): Optional. Specify additional filters to apply. This allows multiple, comma delimeted. Options: IsFolder, IsNotFolder, IsUnplayed, IsPlayed, IsFavorite, IsResumable, Likes, Dislikes
- `IsFavorite` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are marked as favorite, or not.
- `IsMovie` (query boolean): Optional filter for movies.
- `IsSeries` (query boolean): Optional filter for movies.
- `IsNews` (query boolean): Optional filter for news.
- `IsKids` (query boolean): Optional filter for kids.
- `IsSports` (query boolean): Optional filter for sports.
- `MediaTypes` (query string): Optional filter by MediaType. Allows multiple, comma delimited.
- `ImageTypes` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on those containing image types. This allows multiple, comma delimited.
- `SortBy` (query string): Optional. Specify one or more sort orders, comma delimeted. Options: Album, AlbumArtist, Artist, Budget, CommunityRating, CriticRating, DateCreated, DatePlayed, PlayCount, PremiereDate, ProductionYear, SortName, Random, Revenue, Runtime
- `IsPlayed` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are played, or not.
- `Genres` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on genre. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `OfficialRatings` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on OfficialRating. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `Tags` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on tag. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `Years` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on production year. This allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `EnableImages` (query boolean): Optional, include image information in output
- `EnableUserData` (query boolean): Optional, include user data
- `ImageTypeLimit` (query integer): Optional, the max number of images to return, per image type
- `EnableImageTypes` (query string): Optional. The image types to include in the output.
- `Person` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered to include only those containing the specified person.
- `PersonIds` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered to include only those containing the specified person.
- `PersonTypes` (query string): Optional. If specified, along with Person, results will be filtered to include only those containing the specified person and PersonType. Allows multiple, comma-delimited
- `Studios` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on studio. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `StudioIds` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on studio. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `Artists` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on artist. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `ArtistIds` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on artist. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `Albums` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on album. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `Ids` (query string): Optional. If specific items are needed, specify a list of item id's to retrieve. This allows multiple, comma delimited.
- `VideoTypes` (query string): Optional filter by VideoType (videofile, dvd, bluray, iso). Allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `Containers` (query string): Optional filter by Container. Allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `UserId` (query string): User Id
- `MinOfficialRating` (query string): Optional filter by minimum official rating (PG, PG-13, TV-MA, etc).
- `IsLocked` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are locked.
- `IsPlaceHolder` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are placeholders
- `HasOfficialRating` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that have official ratings
- `CollapseBoxSetItems` (query boolean): Whether or not to hide items behind their boxsets.
- `Is3D` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are 3D, or not.
- `SeriesStatus` (query string): Optional filter by Series Status. Allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `NameStartsWithOrGreater` (query string): Optional filter by items whose name is sorted equally or greater than a given input string.
- `NameStartsWith` (query string): Optional filter by items whose name is sorted equally than a given input string.
- `NameLessThan` (query string): Optional filter by items whose name is equally or lesser than a given input string.
- `ReportView`* (query string): The report view. Values (ReportData, ReportActivities)
- `DisplayType`* (query string): The report display type. Values (None, Screen, Export, ScreenExport)
- `HasQueryLimit` (query boolean): Optional. If specified, results will include all records.
- `GroupBy` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will include grouped records.
- `ReportColumns` (query string): Optional. The columns to show.

## GET /Users/{UserId}/Items
**Summary**: Gets items based on a query.
**Details**: Requires authentication as user
**Parameters**:
- `ArtistType` (query string): Artist or AlbumArtist
- `MaxOfficialRating` (query string): Optional filter by maximum official rating (PG, PG-13, TV-MA, etc).
- `HasThemeSong` (query boolean): Optional filter by items with theme songs.
- `HasThemeVideo` (query boolean): Optional filter by items with theme videos.
- `HasSubtitles` (query boolean): Optional filter by items with subtitles.
- `HasSpecialFeature` (query boolean): Optional filter by items with special features.
- `HasTrailer` (query boolean): Optional filter by items with trailers.
- `AdjacentTo` (query string): Optional. Return items that are siblings of a supplied item.
- `MinIndexNumber` (query integer): Optional filter by minimum index number.
- `MinPlayers` (query integer): Optional filter by minimum number of game players.
- `MaxPlayers` (query integer): Optional filter by maximum number of game players.
- `ParentIndexNumber` (query integer): Optional filter by parent index number.
- `HasParentalRating` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that have or do not have a parental rating
- `IsHD` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are HD or not.
- `LocationTypes` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on LocationType. This allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `ExcludeLocationTypes` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on LocationType. This allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `IsMissing` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are missing episodes or not.
- `IsUnaired` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are unaired episodes or not.
- `MinCommunityRating` (query number): Optional filter by minimum community rating.
- `MinCriticRating` (query number): Optional filter by minimum critic rating.
- `AiredDuringSeason` (query integer): Gets all episodes that aired during a season, including specials.
- `MinPremiereDate` (query string): Optional. The minimum premiere date. Format = ISO
- `MinDateLastSaved` (query string): Optional. The minimum premiere date. Format = ISO
- `MinDateLastSavedForUser` (query string): Optional. The minimum premiere date. Format = ISO
- `MaxPremiereDate` (query string): Optional. The maximum premiere date. Format = ISO
- `HasOverview` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that have an overview or not.
- `HasImdbId` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that have an imdb id or not.
- `HasTmdbId` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that have a tmdb id or not.
- `HasTvdbId` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that have a tvdb id or not.
- `ExcludeItemIds` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered by exxcluding item ids. This allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `StartIndex` (query integer): Optional. The record index to start at. All items with a lower index will be dropped from the results.
- `Limit` (query integer): Optional. The maximum number of records to return
- `Recursive` (query boolean): When searching within folders, this determines whether or not the search will be recursive. true/false
- `SortOrder` (query string): Sort Order - Ascending,Descending
- `ParentId` (query string): Specify this to localize the search to a specific item or folder. Omit to use the root
- `Fields` (query string): Optional. Specify additional fields of information to return in the output. This allows multiple, comma delimeted. Options: Budget, Chapters, DateCreated, Genres, HomePageUrl, IndexOptions, MediaStreams, Overview, ParentId, Path, People, ProviderIds, PrimaryImageAspectRatio, Revenue, SortName, Studios, Taglines
- `ExcludeItemTypes` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on item type. This allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `IncludeItemTypes` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on item type. This allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `AnyProviderIdEquals` (query string): Optional. If specified, result will be filtered to contain only items which match at least one of the specified IDs. Each provider ID must be in the form 'prov.id', e.g. 'imdb.tt123456'. This allows multiple, comma delimeted value pairs.
- `Filters` (query string): Optional. Specify additional filters to apply. This allows multiple, comma delimeted. Options: IsFolder, IsNotFolder, IsUnplayed, IsPlayed, IsFavorite, IsResumable, Likes, Dislikes
- `IsFavorite` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are marked as favorite, or not.
- `IsMovie` (query boolean): Optional filter for movies.
- `IsSeries` (query boolean): Optional filter for movies.
- `IsNews` (query boolean): Optional filter for news.
- `IsKids` (query boolean): Optional filter for kids.
- `IsSports` (query boolean): Optional filter for sports.
- `MediaTypes` (query string): Optional filter by MediaType. Allows multiple, comma delimited.
- `ImageTypes` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on those containing image types. This allows multiple, comma delimited.
- `SortBy` (query string): Optional. Specify one or more sort orders, comma delimeted. Options: Album, AlbumArtist, Artist, Budget, CommunityRating, CriticRating, DateCreated, DatePlayed, PlayCount, PremiereDate, ProductionYear, SortName, Random, Revenue, Runtime
- `IsPlayed` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are played, or not.
- `Genres` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on genre. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `OfficialRatings` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on OfficialRating. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `Tags` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on tag. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `Years` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on production year. This allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `EnableImages` (query boolean): Optional, include image information in output
- `EnableUserData` (query boolean): Optional, include user data
- `ImageTypeLimit` (query integer): Optional, the max number of images to return, per image type
- `EnableImageTypes` (query string): Optional. The image types to include in the output.
- `Person` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered to include only those containing the specified person.
- `PersonIds` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered to include only those containing the specified person.
- `PersonTypes` (query string): Optional. If specified, along with Person, results will be filtered to include only those containing the specified person and PersonType. Allows multiple, comma-delimited
- `Studios` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on studio. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `StudioIds` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on studio. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `Artists` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on artist. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `ArtistIds` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on artist. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `Albums` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on album. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `Ids` (query string): Optional. If specific items are needed, specify a list of item id's to retrieve. This allows multiple, comma delimited.
- `VideoTypes` (query string): Optional filter by VideoType (videofile, dvd, bluray, iso). Allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `Containers` (query string): Optional filter by Container. Allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `AudioCodecs` (query string): Optional filter by AudioCodec. Allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `VideoCodecs` (query string): Optional filter by VideoCodec. Allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `SubtitleCodecs` (query string): Optional filter by SubtitleCodec. Allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `Path` (query string): Optional filter by Path.
- `UserId`* (path string): User Id
- `MinOfficialRating` (query string): Optional filter by minimum official rating (PG, PG-13, TV-MA, etc).
- `IsLocked` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are locked.
- `IsPlaceHolder` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are placeholders
- `HasOfficialRating` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that have official ratings
- `GroupItemsIntoCollections` (query boolean): Whether or not to hide items behind their boxsets.
- `Is3D` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are 3D, or not.
- `SeriesStatus` (query string): Optional filter by Series Status. Allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `NameStartsWithOrGreater` (query string): Optional filter by items whose name is sorted equally or greater than a given input string.
- `NameStartsWith` (query string): Optional filter by items whose name is sorted equally than a given input string.
- `NameLessThan` (query string): Optional filter by items whose name is equally or lesser than a given input string.

## GET /Videos/{Id}/stream.{Container}
**Summary**: Gets a video stream
**Details**: No authentication required
**Parameters**:
- `DeviceProfileId` (query string): Optional. The dlna device profile id to utilize.
- `Id`* (path string): Item Id
- `DeviceId` (query string): The device id of the client requesting. Used to stop encoding processes when needed.
- `Container`* (path string): Container
- `AudioCodec` (query string): Optional. Specify a audio codec to encode to, e.g. mp3. If omitted the server will auto-select using the url's extension. Options: aac, mp3, vorbis, wma.
- `EnableAutoStreamCopy` (query boolean): Whether or not to allow automatic stream copy if requested values match the original source. Defaults to true.
- `AudioSampleRate` (query integer): Optional. Specify a specific audio sample rate, e.g. 44100
- `AudioBitRate` (query integer): Optional. Specify an audio bitrate to encode to, e.g. 128000. If omitted this will be left to encoder defaults.
- `AudioChannels` (query integer): Optional. Specify a specific number of audio channels to encode to, e.g. 2
- `MaxAudioChannels` (query integer): Optional. Specify a maximum number of audio channels to encode to, e.g. 2
- `Static` (query boolean): Optional. If true, the original file will be streamed statically without any encoding. Use either no url extension or the original file extension. true/false
- `Profile` (query string): Optional. Specify a specific h264 profile, e.g. main, baseline, high.
- `Level` (query string): Optional. Specify a level for the h264 profile, e.g. 3, 3.1.
- `Framerate` (query number): Optional. A specific video framerate to encode to, e.g. 23.976. Generally this should be omitted unless the device has specific requirements.
- `MaxFramerate` (query number): Optional. A specific maximum video framerate to encode to, e.g. 23.976. Generally this should be omitted unless the device has specific requirements.
- `CopyTimestamps` (query boolean): Whether or not to copy timestamps when transcoding with an offset. Defaults to false.
- `StartTimeTicks` (query integer): Optional. Specify a starting offset, in ticks. 1 tick = 10000 ms
- `Width` (query integer): Optional. The fixed horizontal resolution of the encoded video.
- `Height` (query integer): Optional. The fixed vertical resolution of the encoded video.
- `MaxWidth` (query integer): Optional. The maximum horizontal resolution of the encoded video.
- `MaxHeight` (query integer): Optional. The maximum vertical resolution of the encoded video.
- `VideoBitRate` (query integer): Optional. Specify a video bitrate to encode to, e.g. 500000. If omitted this will be left to encoder defaults.
- `SubtitleStreamIndex` (query integer): Optional. The index of the subtitle stream to use. If omitted no subtitles will be used.
- `SubtitleMethod` (query string): Optional. Specify the subtitle delivery method.
- `MaxRefFrames` (query integer): Optional.
- `MaxVideoBitDepth` (query integer): Optional.
- `VideoCodec` (query string): Optional. Specify a video codec to encode to, e.g. h264. If omitted the server will auto-select using the url's extension. Options: h264, mpeg4, theora, vpx, wmv.
- `AudioStreamIndex` (query integer): Optional. The index of the audio stream to use. If omitted the first audio stream will be used.
- `VideoStreamIndex` (query integer): Optional. The index of the video stream to use. If omitted the first video stream will be used.

## GET /Videos/{Id}/master.m3u8
**Summary**: Gets a video stream using HTTP live streaming.
**Details**: No authentication required
**Parameters**:
- `DeviceProfileId` (query string): Optional. The dlna device profile id to utilize.
- `Id`* (path string): Item Id
- `DeviceId` (query string): The device id of the client requesting. Used to stop encoding processes when needed.
- `Container`* (query string): Container
- `AudioCodec` (query string): Optional. Specify a audio codec to encode to, e.g. mp3. If omitted the server will auto-select using the url's extension. Options: aac, mp3, vorbis, wma.
- `EnableAutoStreamCopy` (query boolean): Whether or not to allow automatic stream copy if requested values match the original source. Defaults to true.
- `AudioSampleRate` (query integer): Optional. Specify a specific audio sample rate, e.g. 44100
- `AudioBitRate` (query integer): Optional. Specify an audio bitrate to encode to, e.g. 128000. If omitted this will be left to encoder defaults.
- `AudioChannels` (query integer): Optional. Specify a specific number of audio channels to encode to, e.g. 2
- `MaxAudioChannels` (query integer): Optional. Specify a maximum number of audio channels to encode to, e.g. 2
- `Static` (query boolean): Optional. If true, the original file will be streamed statically without any encoding. Use either no url extension or the original file extension. true/false
- `Profile` (query string): Optional. Specify a specific h264 profile, e.g. main, baseline, high.
- `Level` (query string): Optional. Specify a level for the h264 profile, e.g. 3, 3.1.
- `Framerate` (query number): Optional. A specific video framerate to encode to, e.g. 23.976. Generally this should be omitted unless the device has specific requirements.
- `MaxFramerate` (query number): Optional. A specific maximum video framerate to encode to, e.g. 23.976. Generally this should be omitted unless the device has specific requirements.
- `CopyTimestamps` (query boolean): Whether or not to copy timestamps when transcoding with an offset. Defaults to false.
- `StartTimeTicks` (query integer): Optional. Specify a starting offset, in ticks. 1 tick = 10000 ms
- `Width` (query integer): Optional. The fixed horizontal resolution of the encoded video.
- `Height` (query integer): Optional. The fixed vertical resolution of the encoded video.
- `MaxWidth` (query integer): Optional. The maximum horizontal resolution of the encoded video.
- `MaxHeight` (query integer): Optional. The maximum vertical resolution of the encoded video.
- `VideoBitRate` (query integer): Optional. Specify a video bitrate to encode to, e.g. 500000. If omitted this will be left to encoder defaults.
- `SubtitleStreamIndex` (query integer): Optional. The index of the subtitle stream to use. If omitted no subtitles will be used.
- `SubtitleMethod` (query string): Optional. Specify the subtitle delivery method.
- `MaxRefFrames` (query integer): Optional.
- `MaxVideoBitDepth` (query integer): Optional.
- `VideoCodec` (query string): Optional. Specify a video codec to encode to, e.g. h264. If omitted the server will auto-select using the url's extension. Options: h264, mpeg4, theora, vpx, wmv.
- `AudioStreamIndex` (query integer): Optional. The index of the audio stream to use. If omitted the first audio stream will be used.
- `VideoStreamIndex` (query integer): Optional. The index of the video stream to use. If omitted the first video stream will be used.

## GET /Artists/{Name}/Images/{Type}
**Summary**: No summary
**Details**: No authentication required
**Parameters**:
- `Name`* (path string): Item name
- `MaxWidth` (query integer): The maximum image width to return.
- `MaxHeight` (query integer): The maximum image height to return.
- `Width` (query integer): The fixed image width to return.
- `Height` (query integer): The fixed image height to return.
- `Quality` (query integer): Optional quality setting, from 0-100. Defaults to 90 and should suffice in most cases.
- `Tag` (query string): Optional. Supply the cache tag from the item object to receive strong caching headers.
- `CropWhitespace` (query boolean): Specify if whitespace should be cropped out of the image. True/False. If unspecified, whitespace will be cropped from logos and clear art.
- `EnableImageEnhancers` (query boolean): Enable or disable image enhancers such as cover art.
- `Format` (query string): Determines the output foramt of the image - original,gif,jpg,png
- `AddPlayedIndicator` (query boolean): Optional. Add a played indicator
- `PercentPlayed` (query number): Optional percent to render for the percent played overlay
- `UnplayedCount` (query integer): Optional unplayed count overlay to render
- `BackgroundColor` (query string): Optional. Apply a background color for transparent images.
- `ForegroundLayer` (query string): Optional. Apply a foreground layer on top of the image.
- `Type`* (path string): Image Type
- `Index` (query integer): Image Index

## GET /MusicGenres/{Name}/Images/{Type}
**Summary**: No summary
**Details**: No authentication required
**Parameters**:
- `Name`* (path string): Item name
- `MaxWidth` (query integer): The maximum image width to return.
- `MaxHeight` (query integer): The maximum image height to return.
- `Width` (query integer): The fixed image width to return.
- `Height` (query integer): The fixed image height to return.
- `Quality` (query integer): Optional quality setting, from 0-100. Defaults to 90 and should suffice in most cases.
- `Tag` (query string): Optional. Supply the cache tag from the item object to receive strong caching headers.
- `CropWhitespace` (query boolean): Specify if whitespace should be cropped out of the image. True/False. If unspecified, whitespace will be cropped from logos and clear art.
- `EnableImageEnhancers` (query boolean): Enable or disable image enhancers such as cover art.
- `Format` (query string): Determines the output foramt of the image - original,gif,jpg,png
- `AddPlayedIndicator` (query boolean): Optional. Add a played indicator
- `PercentPlayed` (query number): Optional percent to render for the percent played overlay
- `UnplayedCount` (query integer): Optional unplayed count overlay to render
- `BackgroundColor` (query string): Optional. Apply a background color for transparent images.
- `ForegroundLayer` (query string): Optional. Apply a foreground layer on top of the image.
- `Type`* (path string): Image Type
- `Index` (query integer): Image Index

## GET /Users/{UserId}/Items/Resume
**Summary**: Gets items based on a query.
**Details**: Requires authentication as user
**Parameters**:
- `ArtistType` (query string): Artist or AlbumArtist
- `MaxOfficialRating` (query string): Optional filter by maximum official rating (PG, PG-13, TV-MA, etc).
- `HasThemeSong` (query boolean): Optional filter by items with theme songs.
- `HasThemeVideo` (query boolean): Optional filter by items with theme videos.
- `HasSubtitles` (query boolean): Optional filter by items with subtitles.
- `HasSpecialFeature` (query boolean): Optional filter by items with special features.
- `HasTrailer` (query boolean): Optional filter by items with trailers.
- `AdjacentTo` (query string): Optional. Return items that are siblings of a supplied item.
- `MinIndexNumber` (query integer): Optional filter by minimum index number.
- `MinPlayers` (query integer): Optional filter by minimum number of game players.
- `MaxPlayers` (query integer): Optional filter by maximum number of game players.
- `ParentIndexNumber` (query integer): Optional filter by parent index number.
- `HasParentalRating` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that have or do not have a parental rating
- `IsHD` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are HD or not.
- `LocationTypes` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on LocationType. This allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `ExcludeLocationTypes` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on LocationType. This allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `IsMissing` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are missing episodes or not.
- `IsUnaired` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are unaired episodes or not.
- `MinCommunityRating` (query number): Optional filter by minimum community rating.
- `MinCriticRating` (query number): Optional filter by minimum critic rating.
- `AiredDuringSeason` (query integer): Gets all episodes that aired during a season, including specials.
- `MinPremiereDate` (query string): Optional. The minimum premiere date. Format = ISO
- `MinDateLastSaved` (query string): Optional. The minimum premiere date. Format = ISO
- `MinDateLastSavedForUser` (query string): Optional. The minimum premiere date. Format = ISO
- `MaxPremiereDate` (query string): Optional. The maximum premiere date. Format = ISO
- `HasOverview` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that have an overview or not.
- `HasImdbId` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that have an imdb id or not.
- `HasTmdbId` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that have a tmdb id or not.
- `HasTvdbId` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that have a tvdb id or not.
- `ExcludeItemIds` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered by exxcluding item ids. This allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `StartIndex` (query integer): Optional. The record index to start at. All items with a lower index will be dropped from the results.
- `Limit` (query integer): Optional. The maximum number of records to return
- `Recursive` (query boolean): When searching within folders, this determines whether or not the search will be recursive. true/false
- `SortOrder` (query string): Sort Order - Ascending,Descending
- `ParentId` (query string): Specify this to localize the search to a specific item or folder. Omit to use the root
- `Fields` (query string): Optional. Specify additional fields of information to return in the output. This allows multiple, comma delimeted. Options: Budget, Chapters, DateCreated, Genres, HomePageUrl, IndexOptions, MediaStreams, Overview, ParentId, Path, People, ProviderIds, PrimaryImageAspectRatio, Revenue, SortName, Studios, Taglines
- `ExcludeItemTypes` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on item type. This allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `IncludeItemTypes` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on item type. This allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `AnyProviderIdEquals` (query string): Optional. If specified, result will be filtered to contain only items which match at least one of the specified IDs. Each provider ID must be in the form 'prov.id', e.g. 'imdb.tt123456'. This allows multiple, comma delimeted value pairs.
- `Filters` (query string): Optional. Specify additional filters to apply. This allows multiple, comma delimeted. Options: IsFolder, IsNotFolder, IsUnplayed, IsPlayed, IsFavorite, IsResumable, Likes, Dislikes
- `IsFavorite` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are marked as favorite, or not.
- `IsMovie` (query boolean): Optional filter for movies.
- `IsSeries` (query boolean): Optional filter for movies.
- `IsNews` (query boolean): Optional filter for news.
- `IsKids` (query boolean): Optional filter for kids.
- `IsSports` (query boolean): Optional filter for sports.
- `MediaTypes` (query string): Optional filter by MediaType. Allows multiple, comma delimited.
- `ImageTypes` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on those containing image types. This allows multiple, comma delimited.
- `SortBy` (query string): Optional. Specify one or more sort orders, comma delimeted. Options: Album, AlbumArtist, Artist, Budget, CommunityRating, CriticRating, DateCreated, DatePlayed, PlayCount, PremiereDate, ProductionYear, SortName, Random, Revenue, Runtime
- `IsPlayed` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are played, or not.
- `Genres` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on genre. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `OfficialRatings` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on OfficialRating. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `Tags` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on tag. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `Years` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on production year. This allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `EnableImages` (query boolean): Optional, include image information in output
- `EnableUserData` (query boolean): Optional, include user data
- `ImageTypeLimit` (query integer): Optional, the max number of images to return, per image type
- `EnableImageTypes` (query string): Optional. The image types to include in the output.
- `Person` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered to include only those containing the specified person.
- `PersonIds` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered to include only those containing the specified person.
- `PersonTypes` (query string): Optional. If specified, along with Person, results will be filtered to include only those containing the specified person and PersonType. Allows multiple, comma-delimited
- `Studios` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on studio. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `StudioIds` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on studio. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `Artists` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on artist. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `ArtistIds` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on artist. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `Albums` (query string): Optional. If specified, results will be filtered based on album. This allows multiple, pipe delimeted.
- `Ids` (query string): Optional. If specific items are needed, specify a list of item id's to retrieve. This allows multiple, comma delimited.
- `VideoTypes` (query string): Optional filter by VideoType (videofile, dvd, bluray, iso). Allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `Containers` (query string): Optional filter by Container. Allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `AudioCodecs` (query string): Optional filter by AudioCodec. Allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `VideoCodecs` (query string): Optional filter by VideoCodec. Allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `SubtitleCodecs` (query string): Optional filter by SubtitleCodec. Allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `Path` (query string): Optional filter by Path.
- `UserId`* (path string): User Id
- `MinOfficialRating` (query string): Optional filter by minimum official rating (PG, PG-13, TV-MA, etc).
- `IsLocked` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are locked.
- `IsPlaceHolder` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are placeholders
- `HasOfficialRating` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that have official ratings
- `GroupItemsIntoCollections` (query boolean): Whether or not to hide items behind their boxsets.
- `Is3D` (query boolean): Optional filter by items that are 3D, or not.
- `SeriesStatus` (query string): Optional filter by Series Status. Allows multiple, comma delimeted.
- `NameStartsWithOrGreater` (query string): Optional filter by items whose name is sorted equally or greater than a given input string.
- `NameStartsWith` (query string): Optional filter by items whose name is sorted equally than a given input string.
- `NameLessThan` (query string): Optional filter by items whose name is equally or lesser than a given input string.
